\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{calibrate\_offsets()}{calibrate\_offsets()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void calibrate\+\_\+offsets (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{volatile uint16\+\_\+t}]{raw\+ADC\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]},  }\item[{volatile float}]{current\+Offsets\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]},  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{num\+Samples }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Calibrate the current sensor offsets. 

This function calculates the average offset for each current sensor channel by reading the ADC values when no current is flowing. The calculated offsets are used to correct the sensor readings.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em raw\+ADC} & Buffer containing the raw ADC values for the channels. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em current\+Offsets} & Array to store the calculated offsets for each current channel. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em num\+Samples} & Number of samples to average for the offset calculation. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void get\+\_\+idiq (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{float}]{ia,  }\item[{float}]{ib,  }\item[{float}]{ic,  }\item[{float}]{sin\+Theta\+\_\+e,  }\item[{float}]{cos\+Theta\+\_\+e,  }\item[{float \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{id\+Meas,  }\item[{float \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{iq\+Meas }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Computes d-\/q currents from current measurements and electrical angle. 

This function computes the d-\/q currents from phase currents (ABC), theta\+\_\+e, and stores the results in the provided pointers.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em ia} & Phase A current in A. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em ib} & Phase B current in A. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em ic} & Phase C current in A. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em sin\+Theta\+\_\+e} & Electrical angle sine (-\/1..1) \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em cos\+Theta\+\_\+e} & Electrical angle cosine (-\/1..1) \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em id\+Meas} & Pointer to store the D-\/axis current. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em iq\+Meas} & Pointer to store the Q-\/axis current. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily float get\+\_\+linear (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{bits,  }\item[{float}]{slope,  }\item[{float}]{offset }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Convert ADC reading to physical measurement with linear response. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}

\hline

\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em offset} & The offset (volts at zero). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{get\_temperature()}{get\_temperature()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily float get\+\_\+temperature (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{bits,  }\item[{const float}]{temp\+LUT\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Retrieves temperature from a lookup table based on ADC bits. 

This function retrieves temperature from a lookup table based on the ADC bits. The lookup table (LUT) must have a value for each possible ADC bit combination.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em bits} & ADC reading converted to bits. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em temp\+LUT} & Lookup table containing temperature values. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Temperature corresponding to the provided ADC bits. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
